

import numpy as np

def is_floats(x) -> bool:
    # check if it is float; List[float]; Tuple[float]
    if isinstance(x, float):
        return True
    if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)):
        return all(isinstance(i, float) for i in x)
    if isinstance(x, np.ndarray):
        return x.dtype == np.float64 or x.dtype == np.float32
    return False


def assertion(out, exp, atol):
    exact_match = out == exp

    if atol == 0 and is_floats(exp):
        atol = 1e-6
    if not exact_match and atol != 0:
        assert np.allclose(out, exp, rtol=1e-07, atol=atol)
    else:
        assert exact_match

import numpy as np

def is_floats(x) -> bool:
    # check if it is float; List[float]; Tuple[float]
    if isinstance(x, float):
        return True
    if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)):
        return all(isinstance(i, float) for i in x)
    if isinstance(x, np.ndarray):
        return x.dtype == np.float64 or x.dtype == np.float32
    return False


def assertion(out, exp, atol):
    exact_match = out == exp

    if atol == 0 and is_floats(exp):
        atol = 1e-6
    if not exact_match and atol != 0:
        assert np.allclose(out, exp, rtol=1e-07, atol=atol)
    else:
        assert exact_match

    inputs = [[2], [3], [4], [8], [10], [5], [6], [12], [15], [20], [1], [25], [7], [100], [500], [24], [101], [14], [99], [23], [19], [47], [48], [46], [26], [499], [27], [98], [28], [18], [45], [498], [13], [102], [11], [17], [501], [68], [21], [30], [10000], [987654], [1000], [1002], [97], [9999], [987653], [22], [29], [10001], [16], [31], [9998], [89], [44], [9997], [1003], [83], [43], [84], [100000], [1000000000], [59], [58], [999], [987652], [998], [57], [997], [996], [56], [9], [55], [92], [50], [42], [54], [53], [87]]

import numpy as np

def is_floats(x) -> bool:
    # check if it is float; List[float]; Tuple[float]
    if isinstance(x, float):
        return True
    if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)):
        return all(isinstance(i, float) for i in x)
    if isinstance(x, np.ndarray):
        return x.dtype == np.float64 or x.dtype == np.float32
    return False


def assertion(out, exp, atol):
    exact_match = out == exp

    if atol == 0 and is_floats(exp):
        atol = 1e-6
    if not exact_match and atol != 0:
        assert np.allclose(out, exp, rtol=1e-07, atol=atol)
    else:
        assert exact_match

import numpy as np

def is_floats(x) -> bool:
    # check if it is float; List[float]; Tuple[float]
    if isinstance(x, float):
        return True
    if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)):
        return all(isinstance(i, float) for i in x)
    if isinstance(x, np.ndarray):
        return x.dtype == np.float64 or x.dtype == np.float32
    return False


def assertion(out, exp, atol):
    exact_match = out == exp

    if atol == 0 and is_floats(exp):
        atol = 1e-6
    if not exact_match and atol != 0:
        assert np.allclose(out, exp, rtol=1e-07, atol=atol)
    else:
        assert exact_match

import numpy as np

def is_floats(x) -> bool:
    # check if it is float; List[float]; Tuple[float]
    if isinstance(x, float):
        return True
    if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)):
        return all(isinstance(i, float) for i in x)
    if isinstance(x, np.ndarray):
        return x.dtype == np.float64 or x.dtype == np.float32
    return False


def assertion(out, exp, atol):
    exact_match = out == exp

    if atol == 0 and is_floats(exp):
        atol = 1e-6
    if not exact_match and atol != 0:
        assert np.allclose(out, exp, rtol=1e-07, atol=atol)
    else:
        assert exact_match

import numpy as np

def is_floats(x) -> bool:
    # check if it is float; List[float]; Tuple[float]
    if isinstance(x, float):
        return True
    if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)):
        return all(isinstance(i, float) for i in x)
    if isinstance(x, np.ndarray):
        return x.dtype == np.float64 or x.dtype == np.float32
    return False


def assertion(out, exp, atol):
    exact_match = out == exp

    if atol == 0 and is_floats(exp):
        atol = 1e-6
    if not exact_match and atol != 0:
        assert np.allclose(out, exp, rtol=1e-07, atol=atol)
    else:
        assert exact_match

    for i, (inp, exp) in enumerate(zip(inputs, results)):
        assertion(candidate(*inp), exp, 0)



import numpy as np

def is_floats(x) -> bool:
    # check if it is float; List[float]; Tuple[float]
    if isinstance(x, float):
        return True
    if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)):
        return all(isinstance(i, float) for i in x)
    if isinstance(x, np.ndarray):
        return x.dtype == np.float64 or x.dtype == np.float32
    return False


def assertion(out, exp, atol):
    exact_match = out == exp

    if atol == 0 and is_floats(exp):
        atol = 1e-6

import numpy as np

def is_floats(x) -> bool:
    # check if it is float; List[float]; Tuple[float]
    if isinstance(x, float):
        return True
    if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)):
        return all(isinstance(i, float) for i in x)
    if isinstance(x, np.ndarray):
        return x.dtype == np.float64 or x.dtype == np.float32
    return False


def assertion(out, exp, atol):
    exact_match = out == exp

    if atol == 0 and is_floats(exp):
        atol = 1e-6
    if not exact_match and atol != 0:
        assert np.allclose(out, exp, rtol=1e-07, atol=atol)
    else:
        assert exact_match

import numpy as np

def is_floats(x) -> bool:
    # check if it is float; List[float]; Tuple[float]
    if isinstance(x, float):
        return True
    if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)):
        return all(isinstance(i, float) for i in x)
    if isinstance(x, np.ndarray):
        return x.dtype == np.float64 or x.dtype == np.float32
    return False


def assertion(out, exp, atol):
    exact_match = out == exp

    if atol == 0 and is_floats(exp):
        atol = 1e-6
    if not exact_match and atol != 0:
        assert np.allclose(out, exp, rtol=1e-07, atol=atol)
    else:
        assert exact_match

import numpy as np

def is_floats(x) -> bool:
    # check if it is float; List[float]; Tuple[float]
    if isinstance(x, float):
        return True
    if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)):
        return all(isinstance(i, float) for i in x)
    if isinstance(x, np.ndarray):
        return x.dtype == np.float64 or x.dtype == np.float32
    return False


def assertion(out, exp, atol):
    exact_match = out == exp

    if atol == 0 and is_floats(exp):
        atol = 1e-6
    if not exact_match and atol != 0:
        assert np.allclose(out, exp, rtol=1e-07, atol=atol)
    else:
        assert exact_match
